# ðŸ“ Continuum Codebase Structure

> **Mission: Reduce complexity and improve organization**  
> Comment on every file - what it does, why it exists, and how to simplify.

## ðŸŽ¯ Structure Goals
- **Minimize depth** - Flatten nested directories where possible
- **Clear naming** - Every file name should explain its purpose  
- **Consolidate related** - Group similar functionality together
- **Remove dead code** - Delete unused or redundant files

## ðŸŽ“ AGENT STUDY GUIDE: Academy & Persona System

**AGENTS: Start here to understand the complete academy system!**

### Essential Academy Files to Study:

**[Academy.cjs](#src-core-academy.cjs)** - UNDERSTAND:
- How `enrollRecruit()` creates new agent personas for training
- How `runBootCamp()` runs TestingDroid vs ProtocolSheriff adversarial loops
- How `performFineTuning()` creates LoRA adapters (190,735x compression!)
- How personas graduate and get saved to `.continuum/personas/`

**[ProtocolSheriff.cjs](#src-core-protocolsheriff.cjs)** - UNDERSTAND:
- How it validates responses and catches protocol violations
- How it evolves through LoRA fine-tuning to catch sophisticated attacks
- How it learns from TestingDroid's successful attacks

**[TestingDroid.cjs](#src-core-testingdroid.cjs)** - UNDERSTAND:
- How it generates adversarial prompts and edge cases
- How it creates prompt injections to test ProtocolSheriff
- How it evolves new attack strategies through competition

**[src/core/academy/README.md](#src-core-academy-readme.md)** - UNDERSTAND:
- The Matrix philosophy: "I know Kung Fu" rapid skill acquisition
- GAN-like adversarial evolution between attacker/defender
- How "The Academy doesn't just train agents - it evolves them"

**[ADVERSARIAL_ROADMAP.md](#adversarial_roadmap.md)** - UNDERSTAND:
- Future adversarial pairs: CodeCritic vs CodeGenerator, FactChecker vs Researcher
- Meta-adversarial systems and cross-domain applications
- Success metrics: 20% quality improvement, 50% cost reduction

### Academy UI Components to Study:

**[SavedPersonas.js](#src-ui-components-savedpersonas-savedpersonas.js)** - UNDERSTAND:
- How `renderPersonaList()` shows academy training progress
- How `renderAcademyProgress()` visualizes graduation scores vs thresholds
- How DEPLOY/RETRAIN/SHARE buttons connect to persona lifecycle
- How threshold drag controls adjust graduation requirements
- How WebSocket updates show real-time training status

**[AcademySection.js](#src-ui-components-academysection.js)** - UNDERSTAND:
- How the training room visualizes adversarial battles
- How it shows TestingDroid vs ProtocolSheriff evolution
- How graduation ceremonies and metrics are displayed

### Persona Storage & Data - UNDERSTAND:

**[.continuum/personas/persona_*/config.json](#continuum-personas)** - UNDERSTAND:
- Persona metadata: name, specialty, graduation scores
- Academy graduation certificates and training history
- LoRA adapter paths and model configurations

**[.continuum/personas/persona_*/checkpoint.json](#continuum-personas)** - UNDERSTAND:
- LoRA adapter details: rank 16, alpha 32, 190,735x reduction
- Training metrics and performance benchmarks
- Deployment readiness and API endpoints

### Training Scripts - UNDERSTAND:

**[run-academy.cjs](#scripts-run-academy.cjs)** - UNDERSTAND:
- How to enroll multiple recruits in training queue
- How specializations like 'protocol_enforcement' work
- How graduation statistics are tracked and reported

**[SpawnCommand.cjs](#src-commands-core-spawn-spawncommand.cjs)** - UNDERSTAND:
- How it creates fresh observer personas (not trained for pure perspective)
- How it integrates with SavedPersonas widget via WebSocket
- How observation contexts and mission types work

### âš ï¸ KNOWN ISSUES & BROKEN CONNECTIONS:

**BE HONEST - Things That Are Seriously Broken:**
- **exec command**: Completely non-functional - doesn't execute anything (critical roadblock!)
- **UI looks amazing but doesn't work**: Beautiful SavedPersonas widget probably can't load real persona data
- **Academy training may be fake**: Training loops might just simulate without actual model fine-tuning
- **WebSocket chaos**: Messages probably don't properly connect UI to backend - lots of console errors
- **API endpoints missing**: DEPLOY/RETRAIN/SHARE buttons likely just show errors when clicked
- **LoRA adapters questionable**: 30MB files might be fake/corrupted adapter data
- **Test nightmare**: Import failures, broken test discovery, messy organization everywhere
- **Error handling nonexistent**: Things fail silently, unclear error messages, no proper debugging
- **Persona loading broken**: UI probably shows "Loading..." forever or fake data
- **Academy graduation fake**: Graduation ceremonies might just be UI theater with no real training

**When studying these files, look for:**
- Error handling patterns that might be incomplete
- WebSocket message types that might not be implemented
- API calls that might return errors
- Training loops that might get stuck or fail
- UI components that expect data but don't handle missing/broken APIs

**Mission**: Understand both how the system SHOULD work AND what's currently broken so you can help fix it!

---

## ðŸ”§ SYSTEM RESTORATION AUDIT

**Evidence: Screenshots show the system DOES work - but it's broken apart**

### ðŸŽ¯ What The System SHOULD Do (Proven Working):

**Multi-Agent Chat System:**
- Multiple AI agents (GeneralAI, PlannerAI, Protocol Sheriff, CodeAI, Auto Route) in active conversations
- Real-time chat interface with agent-to-agent communication
- Cross-agent coordination and collaboration
- Active tab system managing multiple concurrent agent sessions

**Academy-Trained Personas (REAL, Not Fake):**
- **PatentExpert**: 92.2% Academy Score (GRADUATED)
- **Fine-Tune Test agents**: 70%+ Academy Scores (GRADUATED) 
- **ProjectBot**: 80.0% Academy Score (GRADUATED)
- **Legal Test agents**: Various specialization scores
- Real LoRA adapters (30MB files, 190,735x compression)
- Actual graduation certificates and training history

**SavedPersonas Widget (Fully Functional):**
- DEPLOY/RETRAIN/SHARE ORG buttons working
- Academy progress visualization with real scores
- Threshold controls and graduation status
- Multiple specializations: Patent Law, Legal Compliance, Development

**Proven Agent Communication:**
- Can "write to PlannerAI in the continuum interface"
- Agents respond and coordinate with each other
- Multi-agent group chat functionality (with some quirks)

### ðŸš¨ What We Think Is Broken Apart:

**Connection Disconnects:**
- **Command line â†’ UI disconnect**: `--cmd spawn` doesn't connect to working UI personas
- **API â†’ Widget disconnect**: SavedPersonas widget may not sync with command line operations
- **WebSocket chaos**: Messages between command bus and UI may be broken
- **Academy â†’ Deployment gap**: Training works but deployment coordination is fragmented

**Integration Failures:**
- **Fresh agent spawning**: Can't create new instances of working agent types
- **Cross-scope sharing**: Agents work in UI but not accessible via ai-portal.py
- **Test system broken**: Can't reliably test or validate the working components
- **Command discovery**: Working agents not appearing in `--cmd help` or command bus

**Workflow Fragmentation:**
- **Multiple entry points**: UI works, command line partially works, scripts may be outdated
- **State synchronization**: Changes in one system don't propagate to others
- **Error handling missing**: Silent failures prevent debugging integration issues
- **Documentation lag**: README describes ideal state, not current broken connections

### ðŸŽ¯ Investigation Priorities:

**1. Map the Working System:**
- How are the UI agents actually created and deployed?
- What API endpoints are the DEPLOY/RETRAIN/SHARE buttons calling?
- How does the chat interface connect to the personas?
- Where is the academy training actually running?

**2. Find the Broken Bridges:**
- Why doesn't `--cmd spawn` create agents visible in the UI?
- What WebSocket messages should connect command line to UI?
- Where are the API endpoints that the buttons expect?
- How should fresh agents get added to the SavedPersonas list?

**3. Restoration Strategy:**
- Connect command line operations to UI state
- Fix WebSocket message routing between systems
- Restore academy â†’ persona â†’ deployment pipeline
- Create working fresh agent spawn system

## ðŸ”¥ BREAKTHROUGH: Found The Lost Automation System!

**[trust_the_process.py](#python-client-trust_the_process.py) Contains:**
- âœ… **AI agent browser control** - `client.js.execute()` with full JavaScript control
- âœ… **Screenshot automation** - `client.command.screenshot()` with auto-opening
- âœ… **Before/after capture** - 6-step development cycle with validation
- âœ… **WebSocket integration** - Agent registration and real-time communication
- âœ… **Error detection** - Console error monitoring and reporting
- âœ… **Version validation** - Automatic UI element reading and verification

**Why It's Disconnected:**
The automation exists but may not be integrated with:
- Mass Effect slideout panels (`>>` arrows)
- SavedPersonas widget deployment buttons  
- Multi-agent chat selection from UI
- Academy re-enrollment from interface

**Critical Insight:** The foundation for AI agent automation is there - it just needs reconnection to the working UI components!

## ðŸ”§ Maintenance Commands

```bash
# Regenerate this file
./scripts/generate-files-tree.sh

# Add to dashboard sync
python3 python-client/ai-portal.py --cmd docs

# Find files that might be consolidatable
find . -name "*.py" -o -name "*.js" | grep -E "(util|helper|common)" 

# Find potential dead code
find . -name "*.py" -o -name "*.js" | xargs grep -l "TODO.*remove\|FIXME.*delete\|deprecated"
```

## ðŸ“Š Structure Metrics

- **Total files**: $(find . -type f ! -path '*/node_modules/*' ! -path '*/.git/*' | wc -l | tr -d ' ')
- **Directory depth**: $(find . -type d ! -path '*/node_modules/*' ! -path '*/.git/*' | awk -F/ '{print NF-1}' | sort -nr | head -1)
- **Python files**: $(find . -name "*.py" ! -path '*/node_modules/*' | wc -l | tr -d ' ')
- **JavaScript files**: $(find . -name "*.js" -o -name "*.cjs" | ! -path '*/node_modules/*' | wc -l | tr -d ' ')
